\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{   pixels are represented by integers, which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{   must be 32 bits wide or more.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{   True colors are represented as follows:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{   }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{   ARGB}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{   Where 'A' (alpha channel) occupies only the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{   LOWER 7 BITS of the MSB. This very small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{   loss of alpha channel resolution allows gd 2.x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{   to keep backwards compatibility by allowing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{   signed integers to be used to represent colors,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00941}00941 \textcolor{comment}{/* Converts a truecolor image to a palette-\/based image,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00942}00942 \textcolor{comment}{   using a high-\/quality two-\/pass quantization routine}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00943}00943 \textcolor{comment}{   which attempts to preserve alpha channel information}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00944}00944 \textcolor{comment}{   as well as R/G/B color information when creating}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00945}00945 \textcolor{comment}{   a palette. If ditherFlag is set, the image will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00946}00946 \textcolor{comment}{   dithered to approximate colors better, at the expense}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00947}00947 \textcolor{comment}{   of some obvious "{}speckling."{} colorsWanted can be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00948}00948 \textcolor{comment}{   anything up to 256. If the original source image}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00949}00949 \textcolor{comment}{   includes photographic information or anything that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00950}00950 \textcolor{comment}{   came out of a JPEG, 256 is strongly recommended.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00951}00951 \textcolor{comment}{   }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00952}00952 \textcolor{comment}{   Better yet, don't use these function -\/-\/ write real}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00953}00953 \textcolor{comment}{   truecolor PNGs and JPEGs. The disk space gain of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00954}00954 \textcolor{comment}{   conversion to palette is not great (for small images}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00955}00955 \textcolor{comment}{   it can be negative) and the quality loss is ugly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00956}00956 \textcolor{comment}{   }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00957}00957 \textcolor{comment}{   DIFFERENCES: gdImageCreatePaletteFromTrueColor creates and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00958}00958 \textcolor{comment}{   returns a new image. gdImageTrueColorToPalette modifies}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00959}00959 \textcolor{comment}{   an existing image, and the truecolor pixels are discarded.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00960}00960 \textcolor{comment}{   }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00961}00961 \textcolor{comment}{   gdImageTrueColorToPalette() returns TRUE on success, FALSE on failure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l00962}00962 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01151}01151 \textcolor{comment}{/* Style is a bitwise OR ( | operator ) of these.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01152}01152 \textcolor{comment}{   gdArc and gdChord are mutually exclusive;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01153}01153 \textcolor{comment}{   gdChord just connects the starting and ending}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01154}01154 \textcolor{comment}{   angles with a straight line, while gdArc produces}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01155}01155 \textcolor{comment}{   a rounded edge. gdPie is a synonym for gdArc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01156}01156 \textcolor{comment}{   gdNoFill indicates that the arc or chord should be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01157}01157 \textcolor{comment}{   outlined, not filled. gdEdged, used together with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01158}01158 \textcolor{comment}{   gdNoFill, indicates that the beginning and ending}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01159}01159 \textcolor{comment}{   angles should be connected to the center; this is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01160}01160 \textcolor{comment}{   a good way to outline (rather than fill) a}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01198}01198 \textcolor{comment}{   floating point operation, but this is not a performance issue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01199}01199 \textcolor{comment}{   on modern hardware, except for some embedded devices. If the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_source_l01200}01200 \textcolor{comment}{   destination is a palette image, gdImageCopyResized is}}
